\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

\def\PY@reset{\let\PY@it=\relax \let\PY@bf=\relax%
    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}
\def\PY@tok#1{\csname PY@tok@#1\endcsname}
\def\PY@toks#1+{\ifx\relax#1\empty\else%
    \PY@tok{#1}\expandafter\PY@toks\fi}
\def\PY@do#1{\PY@bc{\PY@tc{\PY@ul{%
    \PY@it{\PY@bf{\PY@ff{#1}}}}}}}
\def\PY#1#2{\PY@reset\PY@toks#1+\relax+\PY@do{#2}}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
        \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{dcd2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
        \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adadelta}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{binary\PYZus{}crossentropy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{metrics}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{accuracy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{history2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{500}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{shuffle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{validation\PYZus{}data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{callbacks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{TensorBoard}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{log\PYZus{}dir}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{/tmp/autoencoder/encoding\PYZus{}dim\PYZus{}2}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{acc2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} 
                                    \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} 
                                    \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}3}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
        \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
        \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adadelta}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}

        \PY{n}{acc4} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}5}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{6}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
        \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{dcd2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
        \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}4}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{8}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}6}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{10}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
        \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{dcd2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
        \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
        \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adadelta}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{binary\PYZus{}crossentropy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                            \PY{n}{metrics}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{accuracy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{history10} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{500}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{shuffle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{validation\PYZus{}data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
                                  \PY{n}{callbacks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{TensorBoard}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{log\PYZus{}dir}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{/tmp/autoencoder/encoding\PYZus{}dim\PYZus{}10}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{acc10} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} 
                                    \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} 
                                    \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}7}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{12}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}

        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}

        \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}8}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{14}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}9}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
        \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{16}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
        \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
        \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
        \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}

        \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
        
        \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
        \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}10}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
         \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{18}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
         \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
         \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
         \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{n}{dcd2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
         \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adadelta}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                             \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{binary\PYZus{}crossentropy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                             \PY{n}{metrics}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{accuracy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{history18} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{500}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{shuffle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{validation\PYZus{}data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{callbacks}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{TensorBoard}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{log\PYZus{}dir}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{/tmp/autoencoder/encoding\PYZus{}dim\PYZus{}18}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{acc18} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{evaluate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} 
                                     \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{p}{,} 
                                     \PY{n}{verbose}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \subsubsection{Part 2}\label{part-2}

At this point, I realized that I should have assigned autoencoder.fit to
another xtest and xtrain names because I do not to how to recall the
xtest and xtrain values stored inside history2, history4, history6 ...

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}80}]:} \PY{n}{xtest6} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xtest}
         \PY{n}{xtrain6} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xtrain}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}81}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
         \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{6}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
         \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
         \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
         \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{n}{dcd2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
         \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
         \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adadelta}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                             \PY{n}{loss}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{binary\PYZus{}crossentropy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}
                             \PY{n}{metrics}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{accuracy}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtrain6}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{epochs}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{500}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{batch\PYZus{}size}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{shuffle}\PY{o}{=}\PY{k+kc}{True}\PY{p}{,}
                                   \PY{n}{validation\PYZus{}data}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest6}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtest6}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,}

    \paragraph{Conclusion for Part 2:}\label{conclusion-for-part-2}

It performed just as well as the image that had no noise in the previous
assignment. The line graph illustration is consistent with the
plt.show() we made in the beginning of Part 2.

    \subsubsection{Part 3}\label{part-3}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]

          \PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}noise} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}noise}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}noise}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{prod}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}noise}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}noise} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}noise}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}noise}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{prod}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}noise}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{:}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}noise}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}noise}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{shape}
          
          \PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}control} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xtrain}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{float32}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mf}{255.}
          \PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}control} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{xtest}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{astype}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{float32}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mf}{255.}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}139}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is the size of our encoded representations}
          \PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{6}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} 32 floats \PYZhy{}\PYZgt{} compression of factor 24.5, assuming the input is 784 floats}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this is our input placeholder}
          \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}encoded\PYZdq{} is the encoded representation of the input}
          \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{encoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} \PYZdq{}decoded\PYZdq{} is the lossy reconstruction of the input}
          \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{128}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{x} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{256}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{relu}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{decoded} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Dense}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{784}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{activation}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{sigmoid}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{x}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} this model maps an input to its reconstruction}
          \PY{n}{autoencoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{decoded}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{n}{encoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{input\PYZus{}img}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{encoded}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create a placeholder for an encoded (32\PYZhy{}dimensional) input}
          \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Input}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{shape}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoding\PYZus{}dim}\PY{p}{,}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} retrieve the last layer of the autoencoder model}
          \PY{n}{dcd1} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}
          \PY{n}{dcd2} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{]}
          \PY{n}{dcd3} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{layers}\PY{p}{[}\PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{3}\PY{p}{]}
          
          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} create the decoder model}
          \PY{n}{decoder} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{Model}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{dcd1}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd2}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{dcd3}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}input}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          
          \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{compile}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{optimizer}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{adadelta}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}

          \PY{n}{autoencoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{fit}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}noise}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{xtrain\PYZus{}control}\PY{p}{,}

    \subsubsection{Autoencoder on Noise = 50 vs Noise =
0}\label{autoencoder-on-noise-50-vs-noise-0}

At step 85'ish, the autoencoder's accuracy (noise = 50) caught up, the
acc., loss, val\_acc., val\_loss became indiscriminable from that point.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}140}]:} \PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}imgs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{encoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}control}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{n}{decoded\PYZus{}imgs} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{decoder}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{predict}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{encoded\PYZus{}imgs}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{k+kn}{import} \PY{n+nn}{matplotlib}\PY{n+nn}{.}\PY{n+nn}{pyplot} \PY{k}{as} \PY{n+nn}{plt}
          
          \PY{n}{n} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{20}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} how many digits we will display}
          \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{figure}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{figsize}\PY{o}{=}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{40}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{4}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{range}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
              \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} display original}
              \PY{n}{ax} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{subplot}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{n}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{i} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{imshow}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{xtest\PYZus{}control}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{i}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{reshape}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{28}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{plt}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{gray}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}xaxis}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}visible}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{ax}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}yaxis}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{set\PYZus{}visible}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{)}
          
              \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} display reconstruction}
